\n91:     // When the client connection is mTLS, append the client certificate\n92:     // information to the request’s XFCC header and forward it.\n93:     APPEND_FORWARD = 2;\n94: \n95:     // When the client connection is mTLS, reset the XFCC header with the client\n96:     // certificate information and send it to the next hop.\n97:     SANITIZE_SET = 3;\n98: \n99:     // Always forward the XFCC header in the request, regardless of whether the\n100:     // client connection is mTLS.\n101:     ALWAYS_FORWARD_ONLY = 4;\n102:   }\n103: \n104:   // Determines the action for request that contain ``%2F``, ``%2f``, ``%5C`` or ``%5c`` sequences in the URI path.\n105:   // This operation occurs before URL normalization and the merge slashes transformations if they were enabled.\n106:   enum PathWithEscapedSlashesAction {\n107:     // Default behavior specific to implementation (i.e. Envoy) of this configuration option.\n108:     // Envoy, by default, takes the KEEP_UNCHANGED action.\n109:     //\n110:     // .. note::\n111:     //\n112:     //   The implementation may change the default behavior at-will.\n113:     IMPLEMENTATION_SPECIFIC_DEFAULT = 0;\n114: \n115:     // Keep escaped slashes.\n116:     KEEP_UNCHANGED = 1;\n117: \n118:     // Reject client request with the 400 status. gRPC requests will be rejected with the INTERNAL (13) error code.\n119:     // The redirect request to the new path if these sequences were present.\n123:     // Redirect occurs after path normalization and merge slashes transformations if they were configured.\n124:     //\n125:     // .. note::\n126:     //\n127:     //   gRPC requests will be rejected with the INTERNAL (13) error code.
